(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

    (sliced ?o - object)
  )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)

    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous problem file (pf):
(define (problem alfworld-problem)
  (:domain alfworld)
  (:objects 
    agent1 - agent
    cabinet1 cabinet2 cabinet3 cabinet4 cabinet5 cabinet6 - receptacle
    coffeemachine1 - receptacle
    countertop1 countertop2 countertop3 - receptacle
    drawer1 drawer2 drawer3 - receptacle
    fridge1 - receptacle
    garbagecan1 - receptacle
    microwave1 - receptacle
    shelf1 shelf2 shelf3 - receptacle
    sinkbasin1 - receptacle
    stoveburner1 stoveburner2 stoveburner3 stoveburner4 - receptacle
    toaster1 - receptacle
    glassbottle2 - object
    papertowelroll1 - object
    bowl3 - object
    bread1 - object
    cup1 - object
    plate1 - object
    potato2 - object
    potato1 - object
    tomato1 - object
  )
  (:init
    (at agent1 fridge1)
    (open fridge1)
    (in bowl3 fridge1)
    (in bread1 fridge1)
    (in cup1 fridge1)
    (in plate1 fridge1)
    (in potato2 fridge1)
    (in potato1 fridge1)
    (in tomato1 fridge1)
    (in glassbottle2 garbagecan1)
    (in papertowelroll1 garbagecan1)
    (open garbagecan1)
  )
  (:goal (at agent1 cabinet1))
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

    :effect (and (heated ?o))

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT

  )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

    (heated ?o - object)

  )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )

    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)

  )

    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)

  )

    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous domain file (df):
(define (domain alfworld)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types agent object receptacle)
  (:predicates 
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (open ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (clean ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GOTOLOCATION
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?from))
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
  )
  (:action OPENOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (open ?r)))
    :effect (and (open ?r))
  )
  (:action PICKUPOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holding ?a ?o))
  )
  (:action PUTOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holding ?a ?o) (open ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
  )
  (:action USEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and )
  )
  (:action HEATOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a microwave1) (open microwave1))
    :effect (and (heated ?o))
  )
  (:action CLEANOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (clean ?o))
  )
  (:action COOLOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o))
    :effect (and (cooled ?o))
  )
  (:action SLICEOBJECT
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition (and (holding ?a ?o) (at ?a countertop1))
    :effect (and (sliced ?o))
  )
)

This is the previous problem file (pf):
(define (problem alfworld-problem)
  (:domain alfworld)
  (:objects 
    agent1 - agent
    cabinet1 cabinet2 cabinet3 cabinet4 cabinet5 cabinet6 - receptacle
    coffeemachine1 - receptacle
    countertop1 countertop2 countertop3 - receptacle
    drawer1 drawer2 drawer3 - receptacle
    fridge1 - receptacle
    garbagecan1 - receptacle
    microwave1 - receptacle
    shelf1 shelf2 shelf3 - receptacle
    sinkbasin1 - receptacle
    stoveburner1 stoveburner2 stoveburner3 stoveburner4 - receptacle
    toaster1 - receptacle
    apple1 - object
    creditcard1 - object
    soapbottle1 - object
    glassbottle2 - object
    papertowelroll1 - object
    bowl3 - object
    bread1 - object
    cup1 - object
    plate1 - object
    potato2 - object
    potato1 - object
    tomato1 - object
    vase1 - object
    bowl1 - object
    bowl2 - object
    glassbottle1 - object
    soapbottle2 - object
    vase2 - object
  )
  (:init
    (at agent1 garbagecan1)
    (in apple1 garbagecan1)
    (in glassbottle2 garbagecan1)
    (in papertowelroll1 garbagecan1)
    (in creditcard1 countertop1)
    (in soapbottle1 countertop1)
    (open fridge1)
    (in bowl3 fridge1)
    (in bread1 fridge1)
    (in cup1 fridge1)
    (in plate1 fridge1)
    (in potato2 fridge1)
    (in potato1 fridge1)
    (in tomato1 fridge1)
    (open cabinet2)
    (open cabinet5)
    (open cabinet6)
    (in vase1 cabinet1)
    (in bowl1 cabinet3)
    (in bowl2 cabinet3)
    (in glassbottle1 cabinet3)
    (in soapbottle2 shelf1)
    (in vase2 cabinet6)
    (open microwave1)
    (openable fridge1)
    (openable cabinet2)
    (openable cabinet5)
    (openable cabinet6)
    (openable microwave1)
    (open garbagecan1)
    (open countertop1)
  )
  (:goal (in apple1 garbagecan1))
)
